The breakfast is diverse, but it feels more suitable for Chinese customers. There were quite a few aunts and uncles, and they all ate with gusto. There are also many other functional areas.

The only thing I'm not used to is that there are only two bottles of water in the room. If you ask them, they will be willing to give you 2 more bottles. When we wanted to get four more bottles of water the next day, the cleaning lady emphasized that we could only give four bottles of water a day. Later, we went to the front desk to ask, and the gentleman gave us two bottles of water, but gave us the same reminder.

Now when we stay in hotels such as Asia* and Novotel, these hotels have unlimited supply of bottled water. So we are quite puzzled by Howard Johnson's doing this.

A bottle of bottled water is 500ml. Each of us has to drink at least 2500cc a day, let alone going to Siming Mountain to climb‚ãØIs it enough to only give 4 bottles a dayü§£ü§£ Or should I switch to a larger bottle next time? Or provide water dispensers in the hallways? If you are responding to environmental protection, you can try to adjust the above methods to prevent some people from not finishing the drink and wasting it.
